 magar 3 or 4 oktober bihar par baari sabit ho sakate hai
 The Meteorological Department has issued an Orange Alert in the state for the next 48 hours, according to which light and moderate rainfall may occur in areas of Central Bihar and North Bihar including Patna
 haalanki mausam vibhaag ne baari barish kii sambhaavna se inkaar kiya he
 Disaster department also on alert mode? The meteorological department has also shared this information with the Bihar government, after which the disaster department has also come into alert mode for these two days
 mausam vibhaag ke purvanumaan ko dekhte hue patna jila prashasan ne 3 or 4 oktober ko sabhi nijee or sarkari skool or college samet sabhi koching sansthaanon ko band rakhane kaa aadesh jari kiya he

 hamane roosi vaigyanikon ke saath isaki sanyukt samiksha kii he

 yah abhiyaan varsh 2012 ke ant tak shuru hona he

 Due to late arrival, the aircraft could not board
 yatri kaa kahana he ki vah udaan ke liye do minute der se pahunchaa, jisaki vajah se unki jaan batch gai

 in) Under the Lok Sabha elections 2019, the Bharatiya Janata Party has placed bets on MP Devji Patel for two consecutive times from Jalore Lok Sabha seat of Rajasthan
 devji patel ne apane nikatatam pratidwandi congress ne purv vidhayak ratan devasi ko 261110 voton se haraaya
 Bharatiya Janata Party's Devji Patel received 772833 votes
 vahiin congress ke ratan devasi 511723 voton ke saath duusare or 17714 voton ke saath nota tisare paaydaan par hai
 Rajasthan Election Results Live: Know here which seats in Rajasthan are heavy enough to say that this seat was voted on April 29 under the fourth phase
 matdaan kaa pratishat 65
 Has been 66
 saamaanya varg vaali jalaur loksabhaa seat par mukhya muqabla bijepi va congress ke bich rahaa
 However, a total of 15 candidates were in the fray here
 2014 kaa chunaavpichley chunaav main is seat par 59
 There was a 6% turnout
 bijepi ke deviji patel ne congress ummidavaar udailaal anjana ko haraaya
 While former Congress leader Buta Singh finished third as an independent candidate
 is chunaav main bijepi ke deviji patel ko 580508 , congress ke udailaal anjana ko 199363 or bootaa singh ko 1,75,344 vot mili the
 SOCIAL TANA-BANAJALAUR Lok Sabha Constituency No
8 is the general seat formed by merging Jalore and parts of Sirohi district
 is sansadeey seat ke antargat aane vaali vidhansabha kii 8 siton main se 6 siton par patel-choudhary jati kaa khaasaa prabhaav rahata he
 After this, the votes of Scheduled Castes and Scheduled Tribes are also considered to be decisive
 saal 2011 kii janaganana ke mutabik jalaur kii jansankhya 28,65,076 he jiskaa 87
 42 percent share urban and 12
 58 pratishat hissaa gramin he
 19 of the total population there
 51 fisadi anusuchit jati or 16
 45% are Scheduled Tribes
 seat kaa itihasajalaur loksabhaa kshetra aazaadee ke baad se hi anusuchit jati ke liye arakshit seat thi
 In the total 16 Lok Sabha elections held here, Congress won 8 times, 4 times BJP, 1 time Swatantra Party, 1 time Bharatiya Lok Dal and 1 independent candidate
 pichley 3 baar se jalaur seat par lagaataar bijepi kaa kabja he
 Deviji Patel of BJP is a two-time MP from here
 anusuchit jati ke liye arakshit hone ke kaaran yah seat congress kaa garh rahaa
 Former Union Minister and former Governor Buta Singh represented the Jalore Lok Sabha 4 times
 bootaa singh ke varchasv ko todane ke liye bijepi main unke kad kaa koi bada dalit netaa nahin tha
 Therefore, in the 1999 Lok Sabha elections, the BJP pitted former national president Bangaru Laxman from South India as a Dalit face against Buta Singh
 lekin bangaroo lakshmana yah chunaav haar gaye
 After this, Sushila Bangaru, wife of Bangaru Laxman, was made BJP candidate in Jalore in 2004 Lok Sabha elections

 Most of us feel that the more perfume we apply, the longer the fragrance will remain
 lekin aisa nahin he
 The fragrance of perfume has nothing to do with the quantity
 parafum lagane ke kuch khaas niyam hote hai
 Usually we do not know about them, due to which the fragrance fades only after a few hours after applying perfume
 agar aap bhi har roj aisi hi sthiti kaa saamana karte hai to ye jaruri ho jaataa he ki aapako parafum yuj karne kaa sahi tarika pataa ho
 Keeping these tips in mind, if you apply perfume, then its fragrance will remain for a long time
 1
 Do not place the perfume in a place where there is moisture or dampness
 agar aap chaahate hai ki aapke parafum kii khushboo lambey samay tak bani rahe to use bathroom main bhuulakar bhi nahin rakhen
 Both moisture and heat lighten the scent
 parafum ko sukhi or thandi jagah par rakhen
 2
 agar aapaki skin dry he to aapkaa body parafum zyada der tak nahin tikega
 In this case, it would be appropriate to apply moisturizer before applying body perfume
 aap chahen to petroleum jelly bhi laga sakati hai
 
 iske baad parafum lagane se uski khushboo lambey samay tak bani rahegi
 3
 parafum lagane ke baad kai log use ragad dete hai
 By doing this, the fragrance of the perfume disappears in a short time
 4
 It is better to apply perfume to the whole body, to use it on the parts of the body which are comparatively warm
 kalai, kohni kaa andruni hissaa,kaanon ke peeche or gardan par khaastaur par iskaa istemalkaren
 5
 agar aap chaahate hai ki aapkaa parafum der tak apni khushboo bikherta rahe to bhuulakar bhi quality se samjhauta na karen
 You may save some money by compromising on quality, but you can hardly get the results you want
